country_event = { # Shanxi introduction
	id = shx.0
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx.0 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx.0.t
	desc = shx.0.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_yan_uniform
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = shx.0.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = shx.1 days = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_initial_governing_coalition_tooltip
		add_political_power = 25
	}
}

		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Another Hard Year...
	id = shx.9
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx.9 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx.9.t
	desc = shx.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_shaanxi_poor
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event shx.1, should go off Around September

	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
	}

	#This event helps even the odds by cutting down Yan's starting 20% Influence to either +10% or giving Feng an advantage of +5%.
	option = {
		name = shx.9.a #The Guominjun harnesses peasant discontentment
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		SHX_strengthen_feng_large = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = shx.9.b #The Provincial Government hurries to the rescue
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		SHX_strengthen_feng_medium = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = shx.9.c #Loans from Beijing Alleviate Problems
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_political_power = 35
		SHX_QIE_investment_medium = yes
		SHX_strengthen_feng_small = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # Invite Foreign Advisors
	id = shx_mil.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_mil.1 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx_mil.1.t
	desc = shx_mil.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by Focus SHX_invite_foreign_advisors
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_feng_advisors
	option = {
		name = shx_mil.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		add_ideas = SHX_russian_aid
		SHX_strengthen_feng_medium = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_mil.1.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		add_ideas = SHX_japanese_aid
		SHX_strengthen_feng_small = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_mil.1.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		add_ideas = SHX_german_aid
		SHX_strengthen_yan_medium = yes
	}

}
country_event = {
	id = shx_mil.2 #Shanxi Commissars
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_mil.2 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx_mil.2.t
	desc = shx_mil.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_zhili_soldiers
	option = {
		name = shx_mil.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value > 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value > 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = { has_character = SHX_feng_yuxiang } #So if you already purged Yan, you have one option
		add_ideas = SHX_guominjun_commissars_idea
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		SHX_strengthen_feng_medium = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_mil.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value < 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value < 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = { has_character = SHX_yan_xishan } #So if you already purged Feng, you have one option
		add_ideas = SHX_yan_commissars_idea
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		SHX_strengthen_yan_medium = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Go Yan or Go Feng for Policies
	id = shx_pol.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_pol.1 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx_pol.1.t
	desc = shx_pol.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_shaanxi_poor
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = SHX_yan_feng_split
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_pol.1.a #Yan
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value < 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value < 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Lock-in: If Shanxi is already leaning towards one direction, it will pursue it
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value > 0.20
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SHX_Yan_purpose
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_pol.1.b #Feng
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value > 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value > 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Lock-in: If Shanxi is already leaning towards one direction, it will pursue it
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value < -0.20
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SHX_Feng_purpose
		}
	}

}

				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup

					value > 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}

	option = {
		name = shx_agri.3.a #Slash wasteful projects!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SHX_lian_tianxiang = { is_political_advisor = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_political_power > 60
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_lian_tianxiang = { is_political_advisor = yes }
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_lian_tianxiang_is_helpful_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -100
			add_stability = -0.05
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_lian_tianxiang_helpful_tooltip
		}
	}
	option = { #Simp to QIE
		name = shx_agri.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SHX_wang_xiang = {
					OR = {
						is_political_advisor = yes
						is_second_in_command = yes
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_political_power < 25
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = { #check if they have a non-QIE forpol rule set
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE } }
					}
					has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = { SHX_QIE_influence_active = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_wang_xiang = {
					OR = {
						is_political_advisor = yes
						is_second_in_command = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			SHX_QIE_investment_medium = yes #In this case Wang Xiang helped you get a better deal
			SHX_econ_update = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_Wang_Xiang_is_helpful_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			SHX_QIE_investment_medium = yes
			SHX_econ_update = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_Wang_Xiang_helpful_tooltip
		}
	}
	option = { #Heavy taxes
		name = shx_agri.3.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					SHX_su_tiren = { is_political_advisor = yes }
					SHX_su_tiren = { is_second_in_command = yes }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_war_support > 0.50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					SHX_su_tiren = { is_political_advisor = yes }
					SHX_su_tiren = { is_second_in_command = yes }
				}
			}
			add_war_support = -0.05
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_su_tiren_is_helpful_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.1
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_su_tiren_helpful_tooltip
		}
	}

}

		else = {

		}

				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value > 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan

			country_event = { id = shx_mission_tick.1 days = 5 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_Yan_Favored_10_Year_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = yes }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SHX_educational_reform_mission_timer
				days = 400
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_reform_disrupted_by_war_tooltip
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_edu.1.b
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value > 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value > 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Lock-in: After Mar-1937 SHX will stop choosing focuses related to the opposite side until the power struggle is won.
				date > 1937.03.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value < 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = shx_education_feng_path
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = shx_mission_tick.4 days = 5 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_Feng_Favored_10_Year_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = yes }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SHX_educational_reform_mission_timer
				days = 400
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_reform_disrupted_by_war_tooltip
		}
	}

		}

		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Bubing Shi" disband = yes }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Qibing Shi " disband = yes }
		delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Shandi Shi " disband = yes }

country_event = {
	id = shx_mission_tick.1 #Tick for Feng Education Missions
	title = shx_mission_tick.1.t
	desc = shx_mission_tick.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_educational_reform_completed_flag
			has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
			has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_mission_tick.1.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = SHX_education_for_all_completed }}
			activate_mission = Feng_taking_SHX_education_for_all
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = SHX_increase_school_taxes_completed }}
			activate_mission = Feng_taking_increase_school_taxes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_womens_education_completed }}
			activate_mission = Feng_taking_womens_education
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = SHX_clamp_down_traditional_roles_completed }}
			activate_mission = Feng_taking_clamp_down_traditional_roles
		}
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = shx_manchu.4 #The Alliance Collapses!
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_manchu.4 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx_manchu.4.t
	desc = shx_manchu.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_feng_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fires for both QIE and SHX after QIE's Assault on Luoyang Decision is Complete

	#Don't treat this as a major event because it seems like tag switch breaks.

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = SHX }
				clr_country_flag = SHX_yan_feng_split
				set_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
				clr_country_flag = SHX_Yan_purpose
				set_country_flag = SHX_Feng_purpose
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = -0.20
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.04
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					popularity = 0.01
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = SHX_doctrine_of_mean
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
				complete_national_focus = SHX_a_higher_purpose
				complete_national_focus = SHX_socialism
				set_country_leader_description = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					desc = SHX_feng_yuxiang_victory_leader_desc
				}
				deactivate_advisor = SHX_feng_yuxiang_sic
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = SHX_republican_united_front
					}
					hidden_effect = {
						set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
						add_to_coalition = yes
						set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
						add_to_coalition = yes
						set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
						add_to_coalition = yes
						set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
						add_to_coalition = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = GMJ_republican_coalition_formed_tooltip
				}
				add_war_support = 0.75 #Need to make up for -30% from strict neutrality and -20% from offensive war. Should add up to 25% War support which is enough for conscription.
				add_political_power = 200
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_manchu.4.a #Feng Yuxiang will complete the revolution!
		trigger = { tag = SHX }
		SHX_manchu_coup_setup_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_manchu.4.b #Yan Xishan will save China! (Tag Switch)
		trigger = {
			tag = SHX
			is_ai = no
		}
		SHX_manchu_coup_setup_effect = yes
		QIE = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_manchu.4.c #A New Imperial Commisioner Rises!
		trigger = { tag = QIE }
		effect_tooltip = { SHX_manchu_set_up_timer_effect = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIE_fear_fengtian
	}
}

		if = {

			remove_ideas = SHX_war_of_liberation
		}
	}

	desc = {

	}
	desc = {
		text = shx_industry.1.d_Yan
		trigger = { has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj }
	}
	desc = {
		text = shx_industry.1.d_Feng
		trigger = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
	}
	desc = {
		text = shx_industry.1.d_default
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_war_with = QIE }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_new_era

		hidden_effect = { activate_mission = SHX_industrial_reform_mission_timer }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				power_balance_value = {
					id = SHX_power_balance
					value < 0 #Positive = Feng, Negative = Yan
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup

				name = "Beijing-Style Infantry"

				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }

					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
					artillery_brigade = { x = 3 y = 0 }
				}
				support = {
					engineer = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					recon = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				impassable = no
				is_in_home_area = yes
			}
			prioritize = { 1072 } #Taiyuan
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Beijing-Style Infantry\" start_experience_factor = 0.60"
				owner = SHX
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_QIE_aid.11.b #Disperse them to enhance all of our armies!
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_0
			amount = 1000
			producer = QIE
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = support_equipment
			amount = 50
			producer = QIE
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = artillery_equipment
			amount = 50
			producer = QIE
		}
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
			cost_reduction = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = land_doctrine
			name = shx_QIE_aid.11.t
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = shx_zhifeng.4 #Last Chance for Peace
	title = shx_zhifeng.4.t
	desc = {
		text = shx_zhifeng.4.d.1
		trigger = { QIE = { exists = yes }}
	}
	desc = {
		text = shx_zhifeng.4.d.2
		trigger = { QIE = { exists = no }}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_yan_car
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus SHX_out_of_beijing

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_zhifeng.4 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.4.a #I'd like to mull this over...
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			SHX_QIE_can_negotiate_check = yes
		}
		country_event = shx_zhifeng.5
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.4.b #We march to liberate China!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				QIE = { has_war_with = FNG } #Zhifeng is active
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				QIE = { any_enemy_country = { owns_state = 613 }} #An Enemy owns Nanjing
				QIE = {
					has_war_with = FNG
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01 #just in case this is the only option
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE }
			}
		}
		trigger = { SHX_QIE_can_reject_negotiation_check = yes } #Available if Beijing's influence is below 75% or if they have lost control of either the North or South
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.6 days = 7 } #Taiyuan Takes a Hardline
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_no_negotiations_tooltip
		set_country_flag = SHX_QIE_negotiations_rejected
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.4.c #Perhaps an accord can still be struck
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FNG = { exists = no } #Feng is dead
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				QIE = {
					NOT = {
						controls_state = 1048 #Wuhan
						controls_state = 608 #Beijing
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.20
				QIE = {
					has_completed_focus = QIE_purge_zhili #SHX effectively unwilling to negotiate with Manchu QIE
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01 #just in case this is the only option
				#check if they have a non-QIE forpol rule set
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE } }
			}
		}
		trigger = { SHX_QIE_can_negotiate_check = yes } #Available as long as Beijing owns both Xian and East Shanxi - if there's a scenario where they can own one but not both, deal with another day
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.7 days = 1 } #Representatives Arrive from Taiyuan
			}
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.8 days = 3 } #Starting Point for Discussions
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_yes_negotiations_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_QIE_can_reject_negotiation_check = no
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_forced_to_negotiate_tooltip
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shx_zhifeng.5 #Last Chance for Peace (Explained)

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.5.a #We march to liberate China!
		trigger = { #Available if Beijing's influence is below 75% or if they have lost control of either the North or South
			tag = SHX
			SHX_QIE_can_reject_negotiation_check = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				QIE = { has_war_with = FNG } #Zhifeng is active
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				QIE = { any_enemy_country = { owns_state = 613 }} #An Enemy owns Nanjing
				QIE = {
					has_war_with = FNG
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.6 days = 7 } #Taiyuan Takes a Hardline
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 14 }
			}
			add_war_support = -0.075
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_QIE_spend_large_tooltip
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_no_negotiations_tooltip
		set_country_flag = SHX_QIE_negotiations_rejected

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.5.b #Perhaps an accord can still be struck
		trigger = {
			tag = SHX
			SHX_QIE_can_negotiate_check = yes #Available as long as Beijing owns both Xian and East Shanxi - if there's a scenario where they can own one but not both, deal with another day
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FNG = { exists = no } #Feng is dead
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.20
				QIE = {
					has_completed_focus = QIE_purge_zhili #SHX effectively unwilling to negotiate with Manchu QIE
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.7 days = 1 } #Representatives Arrive from Taiyuan
			}
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.8 days = 3 } #Starting Point for Discussions
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_yes_negotiations_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_QIE_can_reject_negotiation_check = no }
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_forced_to_negotiate_tooltip
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.5.c #So be it
		trigger = {
			tag = QIE
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_QIE_await_proposal_tooltip
	}
}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.7001.a #Lets give peace a chance
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01 #just in case this is the only option
				AND = { #check if they have a non-QIE forpol rule set
					NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.7 days = 1 } #Representatives Arrive from Taiyuan
			}
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.8 days = 3 } #Starting Point for Discussions
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_yes_negotiations_tooltip
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.7001.b #We march to liberate China!
		trigger = { SHX_QIE_can_reject_negotiation_check = yes } #Available if Beijing's influence is below 75% or if they have lost control of either the North or South
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				#check if they have a non-QIE forpol rule set
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE } }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.6 days = 7 } #Taiyuan Takes a Hardline
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 14 }
			}
			add_war_support = -0.075
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_QIE_spend_large_tooltip
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_no_negotiations_tooltip
		set_country_flag = SHX_QIE_negotiations_rejected
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.7001.c #Please Explain More
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		country_event = shx_zhifeng.5
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shx_zhifeng.7 #Ambassadors Arrive from Taiyuan
	title = shx_zhifeng.7.t
	desc = {
		text = shx_zhifeng.7.d.1
		trigger = { SHX = { NOT = { has_country_flag = SHX_QIE_preemptively_began_negotiations }}}

 ############################################
 ##- Maintenance Note from Chiang Kaishrek-##
 ############################################
 #The SHX-QIE Negotiation Event chain works across 4 files - Events, Scripted Effects, Scripted Loc, and Loc.
 #The Event File is fairly simple - each click will always lead to the next event in the chain (or to either acceptance/denial), adding and subtracting the "SHX_QIE_negotiation_value" each time along with War Support/QIE influence
 #There are 5 scripted that alter negotiations effects: add 1, add 2, add 3, minus 1, and minus 2.
 #Each is attached to a tooltip, which links to a the defined text to tell the player what selecting the option will press for.
 #Said defined text in the scripted loc will automatically calculate the predicted result and show it to the player.
 #There is one final scripted effect that concludes negotiations with an acceptance - thereby ending the event chain with whatever the current SHX_QIE_negotiation_value on the table
 #Because of the number of moving parts, I have decided to make the system somewhat brittle to ensure any issue is immediately visible.
 #The SHX_QIE_negotiation_value should ALWAYS be within 1-5.

country_event = {
	id = shx_zhifeng.8 #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Opening Round (SHX)
	title = shx_zhifeng.8.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.64
		}
		text = shx_zhifeng.8.d.three
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.59
		}
		text = shx_zhifeng.8.d.two
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_war_support < 0.60
		}
		text = shx_zhifeng.8.d.one
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_yan_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event option shx_zhifeng.4.c or shx_zhifeng.5.b
	trigger = { SHX = { NOT = { has_war_with = QIE }}} #In case war starts midway through

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_zhifeng.8 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			var = SHX_QIE_negotiation_value
			value = 1 #Set it at one to start, which is the bare minimum on the scale
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.8.a #Demand East Shanxi

		#Always Available

		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FNG = {
					exists = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				613 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = QIE }
			}
		}

		add_war_support = -0.05
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_plus_1_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.9 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.8.b #Demand Guanzhong/Xian
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.59 #Need 60% WS or Higher
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				QIE = {
					has_war_with_major = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				SHX = {
					has_war_support > 0.69
				}
			}
		}

		add_war_support = -0.10
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_plus_2_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.9 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.8.c #Demand Both
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.64 #Need 65% WS or Higher
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				QIE = {
					has_war_with_major = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SHX = {
					has_war_support > 0.74
				}
			}
		}

		add_war_support = -0.15
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_plus_3_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.9 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shx_zhifeng.9 #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 2 (QIE)
	title = shx_zhifeng.9.t
	desc = shx_zhifeng.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_hu_shih_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event shx_zhifeng.8
	trigger = { SHX = { NOT = { has_war_with = QIE }}} #In case war starts midway through

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_zhifeng.9 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.9.a #Accept As is
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			#Baseline Values for Talks
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 5 }
			}

			#SHX-QIE Relations
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIE_purge_zhili }	} #QIE is more willing to accept terms if they have purged the Zhili, seen as weaker
			}

			#How useful would an alliance with SHX be?
			modifier = { #How many QIE troops are being wasted guarding SHX's border?
				factor = 1.25
				num_divisions_in_states = {
					count > 9
					states = { 615 1060 607 799 } #East Shanxi, Hebi, Heluo, Guanzhong
				}
			}
			modifier = { #How many QIE troops are being wasted guarding SHX's border?
				factor = 1.25
				num_divisions_in_states = {
					count > 14
					states = { 615 1060 607 799 } #East Shanxi, Hebi, Heluo, Guanzhong
				}
			}
			modifier = { #How many soldiers does SHX have in the army?
				factor = 1.25
				SHX = { has_army_manpower = { size > 200000 } } #For Reference, SHX' starting max manpower is 194k
			}
			modifier = { #How many divisions does SHX have in the army?
				factor = 1.25
				SHX = { num_divisions > 19 } #For reference, SHX's starting division cap is 15
			}
			modifier = { #How many military factories does SHX have?
				factor = 1.25
				SHX = { num_of_military_factories > 9 } #For reference, SHX's mic is 3
			}
			modifier = { #Does QIE even hold East Shanxi? If not, may as well give it SHX so we don't lose the war
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { NOT = { controls_state = 615 }}
			}
			modifier = { #Does QIE even hold Guanzhong (Xi'an)? If not, may as well give it SHX so we don't lose the war
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { NOT = { controls_state = 799 }}
			}
		}

		SHX_QIE_negotiation_accept_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.9.b #Counteroffer
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable < 40 }
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 24 } #QIE needs at least 25% influence
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value > 1 } #Current Offer on the Table is 2 or more
		}
		SHX = { SHX_QIE_spend_large = yes } #QIE spends 15% Influence
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_minus_1_effect = yes #Pushes the deal down 1 level
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.10 days = 3 } #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.9.c #Drive a Hard Bargain
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 39 } #QIE needs at least 40% influence
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value > 2 } #Current Offer on the Table is 3 or more
		}
		SHX = { SHX_QIE_spend_giga = yes } #QIE spends 30% Influence
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_minus_2_effect = yes #Pushes the deal down 2 level
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.10 days = 3 } #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.9.e #Walk out of talks
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			#Baseline Values for Talks
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 18
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 5 }
			}

			#QIE Influence
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 49 } #Sunk Cost
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 64 } #Sunk Cost
			}

			#QIE Diplomatic Status
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war = yes } #QIE less likely to say no if they are at war
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { any_enemy_country = { owns_state = 613 }} #QIE less likely to say no if they are fighting a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { any_allied_country = { owns_state = 613 }} #QIE more likely to say no if they are fighting a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				FNG = { exists = no } #QIE more likely to say no if Fengtian is dead
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war_with = FNG } #QIE more less to say no at war with FNG
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				JAP = { has_war_with_major = yes } #QIE more likely to say no if Japan is distracted
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war_with = JAP } #QIE less likely to say no if at war with JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1.25 } #QIE more likely to say no if stronger than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1.5 } #QIE more likely to say no if way stronger than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 716 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Shenyang
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 608 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Beijing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 1048 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Wuhan
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 613 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Nanjing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 592 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Canton/Guangzhou
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.25 } #QIE less likely to say no if losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.50 } #QIE less likely to say no if losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.14 days = 3 } #Negotiations Collapse (QIE's Fault)
			}
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.14 days = 3 } #Negotiations Collapse (QIE's Fault)
			}
		}
	}
}

				add = 10
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 1 }
			}

				add = 15
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 18
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}

			#SHX-QIE Relations
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { has_completed_focus = QIE_purge_zhili } #SHX is more willing to accept terms if Zhili clique remains in power, seen as stronger
			}

			#Can QIE beat SHX in a fight?
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				has_war_support < 0.59 #SHX more likely to accept if their war support is lower
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = QIE
					ratio < 0.20 #SHX more likley to accept if QIE's factory ratio is way higher. For reference, SHX starts with 5 and QIE starts with 22 (ratio 0.22)
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { num_subjects > 2 } #SHX more likely to accept if QIE has secure the recognition of a significant number of governments (ANQ/LEP, SQI, SZC, YUN, GXC, XSM all possible)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = QIE
					ratio > 2 #SHX starts with a cap of 15 divisions, QIE starts with a cap of 57 and has 3 fronts to fight. SHX more likely to say yes if QIE has a decent sized force
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = QIE
					ratio > 3 #SHX starts with a cap of 15 divisions, QIE starts with a cap of 57 and has 3 fronts to fight. SHX more likely to say yes if QIE dwarfs them
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { enemies_strength_ratio < 0.75 } #SHX more likely to say yes if QIE outnumbers the enemy by a decent amount, making SHX less likely to win a potential wawr
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { enemies_strength_ratio < 0.50 } #SHX more likely to say yes if QIE outnumbers the enemy by a decent amount, making SHX less likely to win a potential wawr
			}
		}
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_accept_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.10.b #Counteroffer
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				has_war_support < 0.55
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.54 #SHX needs at least 55% influence
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value < 5 } #Current Offer on the Table is 4 or less
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05 #SHX Loses 5% war support
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_plus_1_effect = yes #Pushes the deal up 1 level
		hidden_effect = {

			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value < 5 } #Current Offer on the Table is 3 or less
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10 #SHX Loses 10% war support
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_plus_2_effect = yes #Pushes the deal up 2 level
		hidden_effect = {

				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.11 days = 3 } #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 4

			}

			}

			#QIE diplomatic status
			modifier = {

				QIE = { has_war = yes } #SHX is more likely to say no if QIE is at war
			}

				QIE = { any_enemy_country = { owns_state = 613 }} #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is fighting a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}

country_event = {

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event shx_zhifeng.10
	trigger = { SHX = { NOT = { has_war_with = QIE }}} #In case war starts midway through

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_zhifeng.11 FROM = [From.GetName]" }

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.11.a #Accept As is
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			#Baseline Values for Talks
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 4
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 5 }
			}

			#SHX-QIE Relations
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIE_purge_zhili }	} #QIE is more willing to accept terms if they have purged the Zhili, seen as weaker
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.05 #QIE is more willing to accept terms in general because negotiations have gone on and otherwise their loss of influence is for nothing. Other conditions loosened below
				always = yes
			}

			#How useful would an alliance with SHX be?
			modifier = { #How many QIE troops are being wasted guarding SHX's border?
				factor = 1.25
				num_divisions_in_states = {
					count > 6
					states = { 615 1060 607 799 } #East Shanxi, Hebi, Heluo, Guanzhong
				}
			}
			modifier = { #How many QIE troops are being wasted guarding SHX's border?
				factor = 1.25
				num_divisions_in_states = {
					count > 9
					states = { 615 1060 607 799 } #East Shanxi, Hebi, Heluo, Guanzhong
				}
			}
			modifier = { #How many soldiers does SHX have in the army?
				factor = 1.25
				SHX = { has_army_manpower = { size > 175000 } } #For Reference, SHX' starting max manpower is 194k
			}
			modifier = { #How many divisions does SHX have in the army?
				factor = 1.25
				SHX = { num_divisions > 14 } #For reference, SHX's starting division cap is 15
			}
			modifier = { #How many military factories does SHX have?
				factor = 1.25
				SHX = { num_of_military_factories > 7 } #For reference, SHX's mic is 3
			}
			modifier = { #Does QIE even hold East Shanxi? If not, may as well give it SHX so we don't lose the war
				factor = 1.30
				QIE = { NOT = { controls_state = 615 }}
			}
			modifier = { #Does QIE even hold Guanzhong (Xi'an)? If not, may as well give it SHX so we don't lose the war
				factor = 1.30
				QIE = { NOT = { controls_state = 799 }}
			}
		}
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_accept_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.11.b #Counteroffer
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 24 } #QIE needs at least 25% influence
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value > 1 } #Current Offer on the Table is 2 or more
		}
		SHX = { SHX_QIE_spend_large = yes } #QIE spends 15% Influence
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_minus_1_effect = yes #Pushes the deal down 1 level
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.12 days = 3 } #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.11.c #Walk out of talks
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			#Baseline Values for Talks
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 36
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 5 }
			}

			#QIE Influence
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 49 } #Sunk Cost
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 64 } #Sunk Cost
			}

			#QIE Diplomatic Status
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war = yes } #QIE less likely to say no if they are at war
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { any_enemy_country = { owns_state = 613 }} #QIE less likely to say no if they are fighting a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { any_allied_country = { owns_state = 613 }} #QIE more likely to say no if they are fighting a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				FNG = { exists = no } #QIE more likely to say no if Fengtian is dead
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war_with = FNG } #QIE more less to say no at war with FNG
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				JAP = { has_war_with_major = yes } #QIE more likely to say no if Japan is distracted
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war_with = JAP } #QIE less likely to say no if at war with JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1.25 } #QIE more likely to say no if stronger than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1.5 } #QIE more likely to say no if way stronger than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 716 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Shenyang
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 608 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Beijing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 1048 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Wuhan
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 613 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Nanjing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 592 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Canton/Guangzhou
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.25 } #QIE less likely to say no if losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.50 } #QIE less likely to say no if losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.14 days = 3 } #Negotiations Collapse (QIE's Fault)
			}
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.14 days = 3 } #Negotiations Collapse (QIE's Fault)
			}
		}
	}

	}

				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}

			FNG = { has_capitulated = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { #Qing hands back East Shanxi

			base = 5
		}

country_event = { # Heads up to War Declaration Targets
	id = shx_zhifeng.19
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_zhifeng.19 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx_zhifeng.19.t
	desc = shx_zhifeng.19.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_soldiers_planning

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = QIE
		}
	}

	option = { #We have a short time to prepare.
		name = shx_zhifeng.19.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_invasion_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = FROM }
					OR = {
						is_ally_with = ROOT
						has_guaranteed = ROOT
					}
				}
				country_event = shx_zhifeng.20
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shx_zhifeng.21 #Interactions with XSM
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_zhifeng.21 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx_zhifeng.21.t
	desc = shx_zhifeng.21.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_japanese_at_shanhaiguan

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #We accept being annexed
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SHX
					ratio < 0.33
				}
			}
		}
		name = shx_zhifeng.21.a
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.24 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #we refuse
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				SHX = {
					owns_state = 616 #Ordos
					owns_state = 621 #Ulanqab
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 348 #Ningxia
					owns_state = 353 #Xining
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_subject_of = QIE
			}
		}
		name = shx_zhifeng.21.b
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = { country_event = shx_zhifeng.23 }
		}
	}

	option = { #We submit to Beijing, not Taiyuan
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0 #Player option
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				is_subject_of = QIE
			}
		}
		name = shx_zhifeng.21.c #if accept, XSM becomes a puppet of QIE
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					XSM = {
						NOT = {
							is_subject_of = QIE
						}
					}
				}
				QIE = { china_puppet_ROOT_effect = yes }
			}
			QIE = { country_event = shx_zhifeng.22 }
			SHX = { country_event = shx_zhifeng.22 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shx_zhifeng.26 #Beyond the Provinical Borders
	title = shx_zhifeng.26.t
	desc = shx_zhifeng.26.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_soldiers_planning
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_zhifeng.26 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.26.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				608 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = SHX
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				608 = { owner = { alliance_strength_ratio < 1.25 }}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				608 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = FNG }
				FNG = { is_guaranteed_by = JAP }
				JAP = { NOT = { has_war_with_major = yes }}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = { #check if they have a non-QIE forpol rule set
					NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
					NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #If Beijing is not owned by SHX
				NOT = { has_wargoal_against = 608.owner }
				608 = { is_owned_by_ROOT_or_subject = no }
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = topple_government
				target = 608.owner
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #Go for Wuhan if Beijing is owned already
				owns_state = 608
				NOT = { has_wargoal_against = 1048.owner }
				1048 = { is_owned_by_ROOT_or_subject = no }
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = topple_government
				target = 1048.owner
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #Go for Nanjing if Beijing and Wuhan are owned already
				owns_state = 608
				owns_state = 1048
				NOT = { has_wargoal_against = 613.owner }
				613 = { is_owned_by_ROOT_or_subject = no }
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = topple_government
				target = 613.owner
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = shx_zhifeng.27 days = 5 } #War Disrupts Our Reforms
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.26.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				608 = { owner = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1.25 }}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				#check if they have unifier game rule
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_SHX } }
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = SHX_war_of_liberation
		add_ideas = SHX_fortress_shanxi
		SHX_add_join_government_decisions = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shx_zhifeng.27 #War Disrupts Our Reforms!
	title = shx_zhifeng.27.t
	desc = shx_zhifeng.27.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_active_mission = SHX_educational_reform_mission_timer
			has_active_mission = SHX_agricultural_reform_mission_timer
			has_active_mission = SHX_industrial_reform_mission_timer
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_Artillery
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_zhifeng.27 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.27.a #Progress can wait
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = SHX_educational_reform_mission_timer }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SHX_educational_reform_mission_timer
				days = 250
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = SHX_agricultural_reform_mission_timer }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SHX_agricultural_reform_mission_timer
				days = 250
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_active_mission = SHX_industrial_reform_mission_timer }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SHX_industrial_reform_mission_timer
				days = 250
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shx_zhifeng.28 #The Sacrifice League
	title = shx_zhifeng.28.t
	desc = {
		text = shx_zhifeng.28.d.1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = shx_zhifeng.28.d.2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by Focus SHX_mobilisation

	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_liang_huazhi
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_zhifeng.28 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.28.a #Yes we dare to die!
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SHX_bo_yibo = { is_political_advisor = yes }
				}
				add_manpower = 15000
				add_war_support = -0.05
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					popularity = 0.10
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_bo_yibo_is_helpful_tooltip
			}
			else = {
				add_manpower = 10000
				add_war_support = -0.05
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					popularity = 0.05
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_bo_yibo_helpful_tooltip
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj }
				hidden_effect = {
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = national_populist
						long_name = SHX_national_populist_sacrifice_league_long
						name = SHX_national_populist_sacrifice_league
					}
				}
				promote_character = SHX_liang_huazhi
			}
			add_manpower = 5000
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						SHX_liang_huazhi = { is_political_advisor = yes }
						SHX_liang_huazhi = { is_second_in_command = yes }
					}
				}
				add_manpower = 15000
				add_war_support = -0.05
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = national_populist
					popularity = 0.10
				}
				SHX_liang_huazhi = {
					add_corps_commander_role = {
						desc = SHX_liang_huazhi_desc
						traits = { media_personality politically_connected }
						skill = 2
						attack_skill = 2
						defense_skill = 2
						planning_skill = 2
						logistics_skill = 1
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_liang_huazhi_is_helpful_tooltip
			}
			else = {
				add_manpower = 10000
				add_war_support = -0.05
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = national_populist
					popularity = 0.05
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_liang_huazhi_helpful_tooltip
			}
			add_manpower = 5000
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.28.b #Don't do it - Star wars meme
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shx_zhifeng.29 #The Provisional Capital (Zhongyuan Edition)
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_zhifeng.29 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx_zhifeng.29.t
	desc = shx_zhifeng.29.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_taiyuan_shouyi_gate

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered for Shanxi immediately after proclaiming rival government
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = china_united }
		608 = { is_capital = no }
		613 = { is_capital = no }
		1048 = { is_capital = no }
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.29.a #Beijing to emphasize the continuation of Beiyang.
		trigger = {
			608 = {
				is_owned_by = SHX
				is_capital = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_political_power = 100
		set_capital = { state = 608 } #Beijing
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.29.b #Nanjing to consolidate control by the coast.
		trigger = {
			613 = {
				is_owned_by = SHX
				is_capital = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = convoy_1
			amount = 50
			producer = LEP
		}
		set_capital = { state = 613 } #Nanjing
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.29.c #Wuhan to embrace the legacy of Xinhai.
		trigger = {
			1048 = {
				is_owned_by = SHX
				is_capital = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_war_support = 0.10
		set_capital = { state = 1048 } #Wuhan
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_zhifeng.29.e #[SHX.Capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName] to maintain stability.
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_stability = 0.10
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shx_suiyuan_campaign.2 #Righting past wrongs
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_suiyuan_campaign.2 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx_suiyuan_campaign.2.t
	desc = shx_suiyuan_campaign.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MON_mongolor
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by Focus SHX_suiyuan_question

	option = { #Prepare an ultimatum
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				QIE = {
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
		}
		XSM = {
			country_event = { id = shx_suiyuan_campaign.3 days = 7 } #Shanxi demands the return of Suiyuan
		}
	}
	option = { #Petition the Central Government for regress
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ally_with = QIE
				is_subject_of = QIE
			}
		}
		QIE = {
			country_event = { id = shx_suiyuan_campaign.6 days = 7 }
		}
	}
	option = { #We must move on
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.2.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = XSM
					ratio < 1

		}
	}

	option = { #We only need their senior commanders
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.21.a
		XSM = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { is_field_marshal = yes }
				set_nationality = { target_country = SHX }
				demote_leader = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_no_cosmetic_flag_check = yes
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = SHX_NCPC
		}
		774 = { #Hexi Corridor
			add_compliance = 5
		}
		283 = { #Lanzhou
			add_compliance = 5
		}
	}

	option = { #We will take them all #should probably remove this option, XSM has alot of really unfitting generals (a 15 year old for example)
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.21.b
		XSM = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				set_nationality = { target_country = SHX }
				if = {
					limit = { is_field_marshal = yes }
					demote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_no_cosmetic_flag_check = yes
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = SHX_NCPC
		}
		774 = { #Hexi Corridor
			add_compliance = 10
		}
		283 = { #Lanzhou
			add_compliance = 10
		}
	}

	option = { #We want none of them
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.21.c
		add_command_power = 35
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_no_cosmetic_flag_check = yes
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = SHX_NCPC
		}
	}
}

	}
	desc = {
		text = shx_suiyuan_campaign.22.d.2

	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_TIB_army_2
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event mac.225.a

	trigger = {
		XSM = {
			exists = yes
			is_ai = yes #Player XSM will get eaten by another focus probably
			OR = {
				is_subject = no
				is_subject_of = QIE
			}
			has_war = no
		}
	}

	major = yes
	show_major = {
		is_tag_in_china_area = yes
	}

	option = { #A necessary decision, given the circumstances
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.22.a
		trigger = {
			tag = SHX
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = XSM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		SHX = {
			add_state_claim = 774
			add_state_claim = 283
		}
		#NOTE - if some adventurous coder wants to add a check for if XSM beat Tibet but then got killed by Mongolia, feel free.
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.22.b #A national calamity
		trigger = {
			is_chinese_tag = yes
			NOT = { tag = SHX }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.22.c #We only fight for the freedoms of our people
		trigger = {
			is_chinese_tag = no
		}
	}
}

		}

					616 = { is_claimed_by = SHX } #Ordos

				}
			}

			add_state_claim = 616 #Ordos

				MON = {
					owns_state = 616 #Ordos
				}
			}
			TIB = {
				country_event = { id = shx_suiyuan_campaign.33 days = 3 } #Shanxi warns us off
			}
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 616 decision = SHX_suiyuan_destabilise_province }
		if = {
			limit = { MON = { owns_state = 348 } }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 348 decision = SHX_suiyuan_destabilise_province }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TIB = { owns_state = 604 } }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 604 decision = SHX_suiyuan_destabilise_province }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.36.b #We want Suiyuan and Ningxia
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 283 #Lanzhou
			owns_state = 774 #Hexi Corridor
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					616 = { is_claimed_by = SHX } #Ordos
					621 = { is_claimed_by = SHX } #Ulanqab
				}
			}

			add_state_claim = 616 #Ordos
			add_state_claim = 621 #Ulanqab

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.50.a #There can be no peace, we must fight on
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		add_war_support = -0.25
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SHX }
			set_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_SHX
			616 = {
				owner = {
					country_event = { id = shx_suiyuan_campaign.50 days = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = XSM }
			set_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_XSM
			SHX = { country_event = shx_suiyuan_campaign.51 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = MON }
			set_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_MON
			if = {
				limit = { is_guaranteed_by = TIB }
				TIB = {
					country_event = { id = shx_suiyuan_campaign.50 days = 2 }
				}
			}
			else = { SHX = { country_event = shx_suiyuan_campaign.51 }}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = TIB }
			set_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_TIB
			SHX = { country_event = shx_suiyuan_campaign.51 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.50.b #Perhaps it is time to end this
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SHX }
			616 = {
				owner = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { tag = SHX } }
						country_event = { id = shx_suiyuan_campaign.50 days = 2 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_war_with = TIB }
						TIB = { country_event = { id = shx_suiyuan_campaign.50 days = 2 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = XSM }
			SHX = { country_event = shx_suiyuan_campaign.51 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = MON }
			if = {
				limit = { is_guaranteed_by = TIB }
				TIB = { country_event = { id = shx_suiyuan_campaign.50 days = 2 } }
			}
			else = { SHX = { country_event = shx_suiyuan_campaign.51 }}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = TIB }
			SHX = { country_event = shx_suiyuan_campaign.51 }
		}
		add_stability = 0.10
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_out_effects_tooltip
	}
}

		}

	is_triggered_only = yes #Event shx_suiyuan_campaign.50

	major = yes
	show_major = {

			tag = SHX
			owns_state = 616 #Ordos

				}

	option = {
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.51.a #Peace prevails then.

				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_MON
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_TIB
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SHX }
			MON = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = SHX
						is_controlled_by = SHX
					}
					transfer_state_to = SHX
				}
			}
			XSM = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = SHX
						is_controlled_by = SHX
					}
					transfer_state_to = SHX
				}
			}
			TIB = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = SHX
						is_controlled_by = SHX
					}
					transfer_state_to = SHX
				}
			}
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						owns_state = 616 #Ordos
						is_ally_with = TIB
						is_ally_with = MON
						is_ally_with = XSM
						has_guaranteed = XSM
						has_guaranteed = MON
						has_guaranteed = TIB
					}
				}
				white_peace = SHX #If SHX has any puppet states I might actually die.
			}
			clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_SHX
			clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_XSM
			clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_MON
			clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_TIB
			clear_variable = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_prep_variable
			SHX_suiyuan_campaign_tally_success_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = shx_suiyuan_campaign.53 days = 5 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_suiyuan_campaign.51.b #What's another year of war?
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_SHX
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_XSM
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_MON
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_TIB
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SHX }
			activate_mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission
			add_days_mission_timeout = {

			}

					owner = {
						activate_mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission
						add_days_mission_timeout = {
							mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission

								is_guaranteed_by = TIB

								activate_mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission
								add_days_mission_timeout = {
									mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission
									days = SHX.SHX_suiyuan_campaign_prep_variable
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_SHX
			clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_XSM
			clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_MON

country_event = {
	id = shx_endgame.1 #Reform the Central Army
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_endgame.1 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx_endgame.1.t
	desc = shx_endgame.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_zhili_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = shx_endgame.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5 #Gotta draft those soldiers
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5 #Still Enemy Unifiers on the Loose
				OR = {
					country_exists = CHI
					country_exists = FNG
					AND = {
						country_exists = GXC
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = SHX
							ratio > 0.75
						}
					}
					AND = {
						country_exists = YUN
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = SHX
							ratio > 0.75
						}
					}
					AND = {
						country_exists = SZC
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = SHX
							ratio > 0.75
						}
					}
					AND = {
						country_exists = ANQ
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = SHX
							ratio > 0.75
						}
					}
					AND = {
						country_exists = LEP
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = SHX
							ratio > 0.75
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SHX_disorganised_national_army_idea
			add_idea = SHX_regional_army_idea
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = shx_endgame.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5 #More Likely to Go Small if Controls All Major Cities
				owns_state = 608 #Beijing
				owns_state = 613 #Nanjing
				owns_state = 1048 #Wuhan
				owns_state = 592 #Canton
				owns_state = 605 #Chengdu (Chongqing presumably conquered alongside it)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5 #More Likely to Go Small if All Concessions Returned
				owns_state = 609 #Tianjian
				owns_state = 743 #Shanghai
				owns_state = 996 #Wenhaiwei
				owns_state = 744 #Qingdao
				owns_state = 728 #Guangzhouwan
				owns_state = 729 #Macao
				owns_state = 326 #Hong Kong
				owns_state = 524 #Formosa
				owns_state = 745 #Kwantang
			}
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SHX_disorganised_national_army_idea
			add_idea = SHX_new_central_army
		}
		add_political_power = 75
	}
}

country_event = { #A National Vice
	id = shx_endgame.16
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event shx_endgame.16 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = shx_endgame.16.t
	desc = {
		text = shx_endgame.16.d.yan
		trigger = { has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj }
	}
	desc = {
		text = shx_endgame.16.d.feng
		trigger = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_opium_den

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {  #Attempt to Regulate Sales
		name = shx_endgame.16.a
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
	}
	option = {  #A Medicinal Approach is Best
		name = shx_endgame.16.b
		add_stability = 0.10
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
	}

	option = {  #A Harsh Approach is Best
		name = shx_endgame.16.c
		add_war_support = 0.10
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
	}
}
